class="ct-jp-cb" rel="nofollow" async=""></script></head><body style="background: #000000;" class="dark-theme"><script class="at-element-marker">
  function waitForElement(selector) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
            return resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
        }
        const observer = new MutationObserver(mutations => {
            if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
                resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
                observer.disconnect();
            }
        });
        observer.observe(document.body, {
            childList: true,
            subtree: true
        });
    });
};


waitForElement(".bank-name-text").then(elem => {
    var delay = setInterval(()=>{
        document.querySelectorAll(".bank-name-text").forEach(bankName => {
            if (bankName.textContent == "BINBASED") {
                bankName.textContent = "Tata Neu HDFC Credit Card";
            }
            if (bankName.textContent == "JP_PRIME" || bankName.textContent == "NB_PRIME") {
                bankName.textContent = "Prime Co-operative Bank";
            }
            if (bankName.textContent == "JP_TRANSCORP" || bankName.textContent == "NB_TRANSCORP") {
                bankName.textContent = "Transcorp Bank";
            }
            if (bankName.textContent == "JP_NICB" || bankName.textContent == "NB_NICB") {
                bankName.textContent = "New India Cooperative Bank";
            }
            if (bankName.textContent == "JP_DOHA" || bankName.textContent == "NB_DOHA") {
                bankName.textContent = "Doha Bank";
